      {{#NotFoundException}}Either this profile doesn&amp;#39;t exist on {{tabLongname}} anymore or the profile has been made private. &lt;a class="socialErrorPageLink" href="javascript:void(0)"&gt;Click here&lt;/a&gt; to search for a different profile.{{/NotFoundException}}

      {{#OAuthException}}Salesforce has lost access to your {{tabLongname}} account. &lt;a class="socialErrorSignOutLink" href="javascript:void(0)"&gt;Sign out of {{tabLongname}}&lt;/a&gt;, then sign in again to restore access.{{/OAuthException}}

      {{#APILimitReachedException}}You&amp;#39;ve reached {{tabLongname}}&amp;#39;s maximum number of requests per hour. Please try again later.{{/APILimitReachedException}}

      {{#Service Unavailable}}This feature is temporarily unavailable. Please try again later.{{/Service Unavailable}}

      {{#CSRFException}}The action you performed was invalid for your session. Please refresh your page and try again.{{/CSRFException}}

      {{#InternalServerException}}An internal server error has occurred{{/InternalServerException}}
      
      {{#BadInputException}}{{tabLongname}} search in Salesforce works with names only. You can't use the * character. Please try your search again.{{/BadInputException}}

    &lt;/div&gt;

    {{^noOAuthRequired}}
    &lt;a href="javascript:void(0)" class="socialSignOutLink"&gt;Sign Out of {{tabLongname}}&lt;/a&gt;
    {{/noOAuthRequired}}

  &lt;/div&gt;
</script>

       }
   }
}

    var body = sectionHead.nextSibling;
    var disp = on ? 'block' : 'none';
    sectionHead.style.display = disp;
    body.style.display = disp;
}
